AajurroomiyyahChapter1=umbhalo|of Aajurroomeeyah|e|lolimi|Says|umlobi|Kungenzeka nesihe kuye|Allah:|the izinhlobo|yokukhuluma|umsindo ewusizo:|Ikona|izinkulumo / amazwi|buhlungu nakakhulu,|okunenjongo|ngokulandelana yayo syntactical.|Futhi izingxenye zayo kuphela siqukethe|ezintathu:|Ibizo,|isenzo,|kanye nezinhlayiya|iza|nge Incazelo / nencazelo.|Khona-ke libito|yaziwa|by ukubonakaliswa kasra ngenxa agent|futhi noonation,|nokungena|alef|futhi laam|phezu kwalo,|kanye nezinye izincwadi|kokhuluma of kasra ngenxa agent,|futhi kukhona| kusuka ku- |futhi,|futhi mayelana,|naphezu,|futhi ngo,|futhi nge,|futhi baa,|futhi kaaf,|futhi laam,|kanye nezinye izincwadi|ngesifungo,|futhi kukhona|Waw,|futhi bah,|futhi tah.
AajurroomiyyahChapter2=Nesenzo|siqondwa|nge ngokuqinisekile,|nakubona,|nentando yakhe,|futhi taa|of ubufazi|unkamisa-kancane.|The kuyizinhlayiyana|it|hhayi|Kusho ukwamukela|nalo|zezinkomba zokuthi|zebizo|hhayi|zezinkomba zokuthi|zebizo.|Isicabha|of Ukuphakama kwephimbo|Ukuphakama kwephimbo|Ikona:|uyashintshashintsha|the ngababili|igama negama kula mazwi|umehluko|the esebenzayo element / ibamba|kokungena|phezu kwalo|sobala| noma |ukuzithathela.|Futhi izingxenye zayo|kukhona ezine:|Icala nominative,|futhi icala umenziwa wesenzo,|futhi icala unesikhwele|kanye jussive / icala etshekile,|ke emabito etintfo| kusuka ku- |ukuthi|Icala nominative,|futhi icala umenziwa wesenzo,|futhi icala unesikhwele|hhayi|jussive / Icala etshekile|kuwo,|ke tento| kusuka ku- |ukuthi|Icala nominative,|futhi icala umenziwa wesenzo,|kanye jussive / icala etshekile,|hhayi|icala sebuniyo|kuwo.
AajurroomiyyahChapter3=Isahluko:|Kuqala|izimpawu|of Ukuphakama kwephimbo / icala ophela|Ngoba icala nominative|e|Kune|izimpawu:|the damma,|kanye Waw,|kanye alef,|kanye emini.|Khona-ke|the damma|ke|izimpawu|esimweni nominative|e|Kune|tikhundla:|ibizo|ifomu single,|futhi ubuningi|ephukile,|futhi ubuningi|feminine|umsindo,|nesenzo|samanje|okuyinto|kungekho lutho|enamathiselwe / wathintana|nge isiphetho salo|Noma yini|Futhi ngenxa|the Waw|ngaleso sikhathi|izimpawu|esimweni nominative|e|amacala amabili:|e|plural|nesilisa|umsindo,|futhi ngo|emabito|ezinhlanu,|futhi yilezi:|uyihlo,|futhi umfowenu,|futhi umukhwe umthetho wakho,|futhi umlomo wakho,|futhi labo|yengcebo.|Futhi ngenxa|the alef|ngaleso sikhathi|izimpawu|esimweni nominative|e|ombaxambili|emabito etintfo|ngokukhethekile.
AajurroomiyyahChapter4=Futhi ngenxa|the ngasemini|ngaleso sikhathi|uphawu|esimweni nominative|e|igama eliyisenzo elithi|samanje,|nini|Kunamathiselwe|nalo|isabizwana|of webumbacambili,| noma |isabizwana|of sebuningini,| noma |isabizwana|of ubufazi|ekhuluma / umuntu wesibili.|Futhi ngoba icala umenziwa wesenzo|ezinhlanu|izimpawu|the fatha,|kanye alef,|kanye kasra,|kanye yah,|nokususwa|of the emini.|Khona-ke|the fatha|ngaleso sikhathi|isibonakaliso|ngoba icala umenziwa wesenzo|e|ezintathu|amacala:|e|ibizo|elisebunyeni,|futhi plural|ephukile,|nesenzo|Inkathi yamanje|nini|wangena|kuso|icala subjunctive,|futhi abuzange|Kunamathiselwe|nge isiphetho salo|Noma yini|Futhi ngenxa|the alef|ngaleso sikhathi|isibonakaliso|ngoba umenziwa wesenzo|e|emabito|ezinhlanu,|njengasezindaweni:|(Ngabona|uyihlo|futhi umfowenu)|yini futhi|ezifanayo|lokho.
AajurroomiyyahChapter5=Futhi ngenxa|the kasra|ngaleso sikhathi|isibonakaliso|esimweni umenziwa wesenzo|e|plural|feminine|kuzwakale.|Futhi ngenxa|the yah|ngaleso sikhathi|isibonakaliso|esimweni umenziwa wesenzo|e|the ombaxambili|futhi ubuningi.|Futhi ngenxa|sokususwa|we ngasemini|ngaleso sikhathi|isibonakaliso|ngoba icala umenziwa wesenzo|e|izenzo|ezinhlanu|okuyinto|ipotimende layo nominative|ne njalo|of the emini.|Futhi ngoba icala genitive|ezintathu|izimpawu:|the kasra,|kanye yah,|kanye fatha.|Khona-ke|the kasra|ngaleso sikhathi|isibonakaliso|esimweni genitive|e|ezintathu|amacala:|e|ibizo|elisebunyeni|inflected ngokugcwele,|futhi plural|ephukile|inflected ngokugcwele,|futhi ngo|plural|of ubufazi|kuzwakale.|Futhi ngenxa|the yah|ngaleso sikhathi|isibonakaliso|esimweni genitive|e|ezintathu|amacala:|e|emabito|ezinhlanu,|futhi ngo|webumbacambili|futhi plural.
AajurroomiyyahChapter6=Futhi ngenxa|the fatha|ngaleso sikhathi|isibonakaliso|esimweni genitive|e|ibizo|okuyinto|hhayi|inflected ngokugcwele.|Futhi ngoba icala jussive|izimpawu ezimbili:|the sukun,|kanye kucis.|Khona-ke|the sukun|ke|isibonakaliso|esimweni jussive|e|igama eliyisenzo elithi|samanje|kuzwakale|ophela.|Futhi ngenxa|sokususwa|Ikona|isibonakaliso|ngoba jussive|e|igama eliyisenzo elithi|samanje|ebuthakathaka|ngokuzibulala|futhi ngo|izenzo|ezinhlanu|okuyinto|Indlela yayo|ukususwa|of the emini.|Ukwahlukana|we inflected|the inflected|izingxenye ezimbili:|ingxenye|inflected|ngezibonakaliso unkamisa,|futhi ingxenye|inflected|ngamagama.
AajurroomiyyahChapter7=Bese okuyinto|inflected|ngezibonakaliso unkamisa|Kune|izinto:|ibizo|elisebunyeni,|futhi ubuningi|of brokenness,|futhi ubuningi|of feminine|umsindo,|nesenzo|Inkathi yamanje|okuyinto|hhayi|kuxhumekile;connected|nge isiphetho salo|Noma yini|Futhi ngamunye wabo|wenza nominative|nge damma,|futhi wenza umenziwa wesenzo|nge fatha,|futhi wenza genitive|nge kasra,|futhi wenza jussive|nge sukun,|futhi ahlukaniswe| kusuka ku- |ukuthi|ezintathu|izinto:|ubuningi|of ubufazi|kuzwakale|wenza umenziwa wesenzo|nge kasra,|futhi ibizo|okuyinto|hhayi|inflectable ngokugcwele|yenziwa genitive|nge fatha,|nesenzo|samanje|Kunamathiselwe|isiphetho salo|jussive|nokususa|of isiphetho salo.|Futhi yiziphi|inflects|ngamagama|zine|izinhlobo:|the ombaxambili,|futhi ubuningi|of ngobudoda|umsindo,|futhi amabizo|ezinhlanu,|futhi izenzo|ezinhlanu,|futhi yilezi:|they wesilisa ezimbili,|labo ababili njengabesifazane / kuwe ezimbili|benza konke nesilisa do,|nani nonke nesilisa do,|futhi wena feminine ukukwenza.
AajurroomiyyahChapter8=Khona-ke|the webumbacambili|khona-ke wenze icala nominative|ne alef,|futhi wenze icala umenziwa wesenzo|futhi wenze icala genitive|ne yah.|Futhi ngenxa|plural|of ngobudoda|kuzwakale|ke kwenza icala nominative|ne Waw|futhi kwenza icala umenziwa wesenzo|futhi kwenza icala genitive|ne yah.|Futhi ngenxa|emabito|ezinhlanu|ke kwenza icala nominative|nge Waw,|futhi kwenza icala umenziwa wesenzo|nge alef,|futhi kwenza icala genitive|nge yah.|Futhi ngenxa|izenzo|ezinhlanu|ke kwenza kwemizwa Indlela|imini,|futhi kwenza kwemizwa subjunctive|futhi kwenza kwemizwa jussive|nokususa of it.|isahluko|of the tento|izenzo|yilezi ezintathu:|sikhatsi lesengcile,|futhi sanje,|niyale esishubile,|njengasezindaweni:|wamshaya,|futhi akazange hit,|futhi hit.|The sikhatsi lesengcile|nge fatha|ngokuzibulala|(njalo)|poqo esishubile|jussive|(njalo)
AajurroomiyyahChapter9=Futhi sanje|ini|kwaba|e|yayo yokuqala|one|izithasiselo|Kune|okuyinto|uma sahlanganiswa|ongathi ngaye:|(Hamza, emini, yah futhi tah)|futhi kuba|icala nominative|(njalo)|kuze|engena|phezu kwalo|subjunctive| noma |jussive.|Khona-ke subjunctiveness|eziyishumi,|futhi yilezi:|ukuze / lokho,|futhi ungalokothi / ngeke,|bese / Ngakho,|futhi ukuze / ukwenzela bona,|futhi lam|ukuze,|futhi lam|of ukugwema,|futhi kuze kube / up to,|kanti impendulo / siphetfo / umshwana oyinhloko yomusho|ne fah|kanye Waw,|futhi noma.|Futhi jussive|eziyisishiyagalombili|eziyishumi,|futhi yilezi:|yena akhenge enze njalo,|futhi akazange / lokho,|futhi akazange ashade,|nokuthi yini,|futhi lam|ngomyalo|nangokunxusa,|futhi|(ungenzi)|e|ukwenqatshelwa kokusetshenziswa|nangokunxusa,|futhi uma,|yini futhi,|futhi noma ubani,|futhi noma yini,|futhi noma nini lapho / uma|ini,|lapho,|futhi lapho,|futhi lapho|kanye nanokuthi ukuphi,|futhi ngendlela yokuthi,|futhi nomaphi,|Nokho, futhi|kanye / Ngakho-ke|e|izinkondlo|ngokuqondile.

GreatMasterpiece12=Futhi ngenxa|ibizo|elisebunyeni|ke okuhloswe / wayesho|nalo|lapha|ini|abuzange|webumbacambili|hhayi|sebuningini|hhayi|wajoyina|kubo|hhayi| kusuka ku- |emabito|ezinhlanu:|Kungakhathaliseki|Nginayo|okuhloswe / wayesho|nalo|nesilisa|Ngokwesibonelo:|Muhammad,|futhi Ali,|futhi Hamza,| noma |kwaba|okuhloswe / wayesho|nalo|ubufazi|Ngokwesibonelo:|Fatima,|futhi Aisha,|futhi Zaynab,|futhi sezulu|kade|the damma|ebonakalayo / sobala|njengani|ungaphakathi|isibonelo:|(Ufunda / weza|Muhammad)|futhi|(ngohambo|Fatima),| noma |kade|engabe|njengasezindaweni:|(Ufunda|lo mfana|umahluleli|nomfowethu)|njengasezindaweni:|(washada|ubusuku|noNawomi)|ke uma|(Muhammad)|kanye ne|(Fatima)|kukhona kokubili icala nominative,|nesibonakaliso|yecala nominative|the damma|sobala,|futhi|(The boy)|futhi isibonelo yayo|(Ebusuku)|futhi|(UNawomi)|kukhona icala nominative,|nezibonakaliso|cala nominative|kuyinto damma|engabe|phezu|the alef|ekuvimbeleni| kusuka ku- |ebonakalayo yalo / sobala|engenakwenzeka,|futhi|(Ijaji)|Indaba nominative,|nesibonakaliso|icala layo nominative|kuyinto damma|engabe|phezu|yah|ekuvimbeleni| kusuka ku- |ebonakalayo yalo / sobala|nobunzima,|futhi|(ubhuti wami)|Indaba nominative,|nesibonakaliso|icala layo nominative|the damma|engabe|phezu|ini|kungaphambi|the yah|lomuntu lokuqala|ekuvimbeleni| kusuka ku- |ebonakalayo yalo / sobala|vowelling|ezifanele.
GreatMasterpiece13=Ukubuyiselwa|we Waw| kusuka ku- |damma|Ithi:|futhi|the Waw|ngaleso sikhathi|izimpawu|esimweni nominative|e|amacala amabili:|e|plural|nesilisa|umsindo,|futhi ngo|emabito|ezinhlanu,|futhi yilezi:|uyihlo,|futhi umfowenu,|futhi umukhwe umthetho wakho,|futhi umlomo wakho,|futhi labo|yengcebo.|Ngithi:|kwaba|the Waw|izimpawu|phezu|icala nominative|amazwi|e|amacala amabili:|okokuqala:|plural|nesilisa|umsindo,|futhi icala|umzuzwana|emabito|ezinhlanu.|Ka-:|plural|nesilisa|umsindo,|Ikona:|libito|okubonisa / ebhekisela ezinhlekeleleni|phezu|ophela| kusuka ku- |ezimbili,|ngokwanda|e|isiphetho salo,|kuba esebenzayo|mahhala| kusuka ku- |lokhu|Ngaphezu kwalokho,|futhi wajoyina|kuya ukuthandwa|of it,|njengasezindaweni:|(bajabula|labo abasala) (9:81),|(kodwa|labo babo abangamalungu ngokuqinile|e|ulwazi|kusukela kubo|kholwa) (4: 162),|(Futhi uma|zonda / awathandwanga it|izigebengu / enecala) (8: 8),|IF|khona kube|kusuka kuwe|mabini|ngabagxilile) (8:65),|(Futhi abanye ubani|baye bavuma|amaphutha abo) (9: 102).|lapho-ke yilowo|kusuka:|(Labo abasala)|futhi|(Labo babo abangamalungu ngokuqinile)|futhi|(Kholwa)|futhi|(Izigebengu / enecala)|futhi|(Ngabagxilile / isiguli)|futhi|(Abanye)|plural|nesilisa|umsindo,|ebhekisela ezinhlekeleleni|phezu|abaningi| kusuka ku- |ezimbili,|futhi kuwo|i kwalokho|e|isiphetho salo|-|futhi kuba|the Waw|futhi kwaba semini|-|futhi kuba|evumelekile|mahhala| kusuka ku- |lokhu|ukwandisa,|hhayi|bheka|kwakho|wena uthi:|lowo uyasala,|futhi lowo siqinile,|futhi ikholwa,|kanye / elilodwa isigebengu enecala,|futhi isiguli / ogxilile,|futhi enye,|futhi zonke|ukusho| kusuka ku- |izinkulumo|plural|nesenzakalo|e|lokhu|uphawu|Icala nominative,|nezibonakaliso|icala layo nominative|the Waw|replacement| kusuka ku- |the damma,|futhi lokhu|ngasemini|okuyinto|kungemva|the Waw|obambele| kusuka ku- |tanween|e|izwi lakho:|(Umise umuntu onokwethenjelwa)|futhi ube ncono kunaloko,|futhi kuba|ibizo|elisebunyeni.

GreatMasterpiece29=The inflected|Ithi:|(Division)|The inflected|izingxenye ezimbili:|ingxenye|inflected|ngezibonakaliso unkamisa,|futhi ingxenye|inflected|ngamagama.|Futhi ngithi:|ufuna|umlobi|-|Kungenzeka angajabula naye|Allah|oPhezukonke|-|nalezi|ukwehlukana|ukuthi|libhekisela|phezu|ngendlela summarization|wezindleko,|lesi sinqumo|ini|ngaphambilini|it yasekelwa|e|izindawo|of Ukuphakama kwephimbo,|futhi izikhundla|okuyinto|ngaphambilini|obalulwe|izinqumo zabo|e|Ukuphakama kwephimbo|kwenaba|eziyisishiyagalombili,|futhi yilezi:|ibizo|elisebunyeni,|futhi ubuningi|of brokenness,|futhi ubuningi|of feminine|umsindo,|nesenzo|Inkathi yamanje|okuyinto|hhayi|Kunamathiselwe|nge isiphetho salo|Noma yini|kanye ombaxambili,|futhi ubuningi|of nesilisa|umsindo,|futhi amabizo|ezinhlanu,|futhi izenzo|ezinhlanu,|futhi lezi|izinhlobo|-|okuyinto|kukhona|izindawo|of Ukuphakama kwephimbo|-|zihlukaniswe| ku |izingxenye ezimbili:|engxenyeni|Kuqala|inflected|ngezibonakaliso unkamisa,|engxenyeni|umzuzwana|inflected|ngamagama,|futhi lilandela|uthole incazelo|ohlotsheni ngalunye|okuyingxenye|kusukela kulezi|nekuchazwa.

GreatMasterpiece32=The inflected|ngamagama|Ithi:|futhi yiziphi|inflects|ngamagama|zine|izinhlobo:|the ombaxambili,|futhi ubuningi|of ngobudoda|umsindo,|futhi amabizo|ezinhlanu,|futhi izenzo|ezinhlanu,|futhi yilezi:|they wesilisa ezimbili,|labo ababili njengabesifazane / kuwe ezimbili|benza konke nesilisa do,|nani nonke nesilisa do,|futhi wena feminine ukukwenza.|Futhi ngithi:|engxenyeni|umzuzwana| kusuka ku- |the inflected:|izinto|okuyinto|inflect|ngamagama,|izinhlamvu|okuyinto|ngamashumi|izimpawu|phezu|the inflections|Kune|futhi yilezi:|the alef,|kanye Waw,|kanye yah,|kanye emini,|nokuthi yiziphi|inflects|nalezi|izinhlamvu|zine|izinto:|‚Ä¢ %1.|duality,|futhi kuhloswe|nalo|the ombaxambili,|futhi isibonelo yayo:|(Kwala mazwe womabili,|kanye Muhammads ezimbili,|kanye Bakrs ezimbili,|futhi la madoda amabili)|2-|ubuningi|of ngobudoda|umsindo,|futhi isibonelo yayo:|(Muslim,|the Bakrs,|the Muhammads)|3-|emabito|ezinhlanu|futhi yilezi:|(Uyihlo,|futhi umfowenu,|futhi uyihlo umalokazana,|futhi umlomo wakho,|possessor|basuke bengabangane bengcebo).|4-|The tento|ezinhlanu|futhi isibonelo sabo:|(Amadoda amabili hit,|kanti abesifazane ababili / kuwe ezimbili bhala / linqume,|futhi wonke amadoda baqonde,|futhi wena wonke amadoda ukulondoloza / ngekhanda,|wena feminine kukhona becabangela / ngizochitha khona ubusuku / Awaken).|Futhi uyokunika|imiboniso|we Ukuphakama kwephimbo|ngamunye|one| kusuka ku- |lezi|izinto|Kune|ngokuningiliziwe.

GreatMasterpiece35=Ukuphakama kwephimbo|of amabizo|ezinhlanu|Ithi:|Futhi ngenxa|emabito|ezinhlanu|ke kwenza icala nominative|nge Waw,|futhi kwenza icala umenziwa wesenzo|nge alef,|futhi kwenza icala genitive|nge yah.|Futhi ngithi:|owesithathu| kusuka ku- |izinto|okuyinto|inflect|ngamagama|(Amabizo|emihlanu)|futhi ngokuqinisekile|(ngaphambilini)|Bebonga|futhi ubheke|izimo|of Ukuphakama kwephimbo yayo|lokhu|Ukuphakama kwephimbo.|Futhi isinqumo sayo:|ukuthi|ke kwenza icala nominative|ne Waw|replacement| kusuka ku- |the damma,|futhi kwenza icala umenziwa wesenzo|ne alef|replacement| kusuka ku- |the fatha|futhi kwenza icala genitive|ne yah|replacement| kusuka ku- |the kasra.|Bese isibonelo|of amabizo|ezinhlanu|icala nominative|IF|okuyala|uyihlo|ke ukumlalela)|futhi|(ifika|umfowenu| kusuka ku- |travel yakhe)|khona-ke yilowo| kusuka ku- |(Uyihlo)|futhi|(Umfowenu)|Icala nominative,|ke ngoba|kuyinto element asebenzayo,|nesibonakaliso|of nominative yayo|the Waw|replacement| kusuka ku- |the damma,|ngoba ukuthi|kuvela|emabito|ezinhlanu,|futhi kaaf|sinakho|kuso,|ezihlelekile|phezu|the fatha|e|indawo|genitive.|Futhi isibonelo|of amabizo|ezinhlanu|icala umenziwa wesenzo|(ukulalela|uyihlo)|futhi|(love|umfowenu)|khona-ke yilowo| kusuka ku- |(Uyihlo)|futhi|(Umfowenu)|Icala umenziwa wesenzo,|ngoba ukuthi|kuyinto oyibamba|phezu kwalo,|nesibonakaliso|of umenziwa wesenzo yayo|the alef|replacement| kusuka ku- |the fatha,|ngoba ukuthi|kuvela|emabito|ezinhlanu,|futhi kaaf|sinakho|kuso,|ezihlelekile|phezu|the fatha|e|genitive,|Njengoba kunje|(ngaphambilini)|Futhi isibonelo|of amabizo|ezinhlanu|icala genitive|linda okuzayo|Iya ku-|uyihlo,|ukuzwelana / sikhathazeke|nge / mayelana|umfowenu)|khona-ke yilowo| kusuka ku- |(Uyihlo)|futhi|(Umfowenu)|Icala genitive,|ukufaka|the kuyizinhlayiyana|of genitive|phezu kwalo,|nesibonakaliso|of genitive yayo|the yah|replacement| kusuka ku- |the kasra,|ngoba ukuthi|kuvela|emabito|ezinhlanu,|futhi kaaf|sinakho|kuso|Njengoba kunje|(ngaphambilini)

GreatMasterpiece37=The tento|futhi izinhlobo zalo|Ithi:|(Esahlukweni|of the tento)|izenzo|yilezi ezintathu:|sikhatsi lesengcile,|futhi sanje,|niyale esishubile,|njengasezindaweni:|wamshaya,|futhi akazange hit,|futhi hit.|Futhi ngithi:|lihlukaniswe|igama eliyisenzo elithi| ku |ezintathu|izingxenye:|engxenyeni|Kuqala|sikhatsi lesengcile,|futhi kuba|ini|kuboniswa|phezu|kokuthola|izinto|ngaphambi|isikhathi|yokukhuluma,|njengasezindaweni:|(Wamshaya,|futhi wasiza / ekuzaleni,|futhi wavula,|futhi wayazi,|futhi thinked / uthathwa,|futhi wayephana).|ingxenye|umzuzwana|usenkathini yamanje,|futhi kuba|ini|kuboniswa|phezu|kokuthola|izinto|e|isikhathi|yokukhuluma,| noma |emva kwalo,|njengasezindaweni:|(Yena hits,|futhi kusiza esiza /,|futhi ivula,|yena-ke uyazi,|futhi ecabanga / ayibona,|futhi ukuphana).|Futhi ingxenye|Isithathu|umyalo esishubile,|futhi kuba|ini|lelandzelako|nalo|kokuthola|izinto|emuva|isikhathi|yokukhuluma,|njengasezindaweni:|ukutholakala komsebenzi|kanye nosizo / basize,|futhi evulekile,|futhi bazi,|futhi ucabange / sibona,|futhi kube ophanayo).|Futhi ngokuqinisekile|siyamukhumbuza|kwakho|e|ekuqaleni|sencwadi|lezi|izingxenye,|futhi thina ukukhumbuza|kwakho|nalo|isibonakaliso|Lwazo zonke |okuyingxenye| kusuka ku- |lezi|izingxenye|ezintathu.

GreatMasterpiece39=The subjunctiveness|of sanje|Ithi:|khona-ke subjunctiveness|eziyishumi,|futhi yilezi:|ukuze / lokho,|futhi ungalokothi / ngeke,|bese / Ngakho,|futhi ukuze / ukwenzela bona,|futhi lam|ukuze,|futhi lam|of ukugwema,|futhi kuze kube / up to,|kanti impendulo / siphetfo / umshwana oyinhloko yomusho|ne fah|kanye Waw,|futhi noma.|Futhi ngithi:|eqenjini / izinhlayiya|okuyinto|lihlukana|ngemuva kwalo|igama eliyisenzo elithi|Inkathi yamanje|eziyishumi|izinhlayiya|futhi kukhona|ku-|ezintathu|izingxenye:|ingxenye|kwenza ngithi:|amathuluzi|okuyinto|ukwenza kwemizwa jussive|igama eliyisenzo elithi|Inkathi yamanje|eziyisishiyagalombili|eziyishumi|of jussive,|futhi lezi|amathuluzi|ihlukanise|Iya ku-|izingxenye GreatMasterpiece45=The obambele| kusuka ku- |element esebenzayo|Ithi:|isahluko|of ayifeze|okuyinto|wakwenza hhayi|fonela|element yayo asebenzayo)|futhi kuba:|Ibizo,|Icala nominative,|okuyinto|wakwenza hhayi|ziyakhuluma|nalo|element yayo asebenzayo.|Futhi ngithi:|ngokuqinisekile|yi-|enkulumweni|umbhali| kusuka ku- |esenzweni|futhi isici esebenzayo|futhi i ayifeze|nalo,|like nje|nquma|Mahmood|igatsha)|futhi njengawo|(ngizazi ngekhanda|Khalil|the isifundo)|futhi njengawo|(ukusikeka|Abrahama|igatsha)|futhi|(ngengcondvo|Ali|the isifundo)|futhi ngokuqinisekile|sokususwa|sikhulumi / kwendlulisa umuntu wokuqala|timphawu esebenzayo| kusuka ku- |lokhu|inkulumo|futhi anelisekile|nge Khumbuzani|sesenzo|futhi yayo ukuze ayifeze,|kuleli cala / ngaleso sikhathi|kudingekile|phezu kwalo|ukuthi|Izinguquko|ifomu|sesenzo,|kanye nezinguquko|iphethini / ifomu|we ayifeze|futhi,|Nge-|Izinguquko|isithombe|sesenzo|ke uyonika|enkulumweni|phezu kwalo,|futhi|Izinguquko|iphethini / ifomu|we ayifeze|ke ngokuqinisekile|emuva|ukuthi|kwaba|icala umenziwa wesenzo|kuba|Icala nominative,|futhi unikezwa|lesi sinqumo|timphawu esebenzayo:| kusuka ku- |yesidingo|ngokulibala| kusuka ku- |isenzo,|kanye ubufazi|sesenzo|ngoba|IF|kwaba|feminine,|kanye nezinye kuka|ukuthi,|namakholi|ngaleso sizathu|(kufakwe|timphawu esebenzayo)| noma |(The ayifeze|okuyinto|wakwenza hhayi|fonela|element yayo asebenzayo).
GreatMasterpiece46=Izinguquko kungelokothe kwenzeke|igama eliyisenzo elithi|emuva|ukusulwa|timphawu esebenzayo|Ithi:|ke uma|kwaba|igama eliyisenzo elithi|sikhatsi lesengcile|wafaka damma|okokuqala|wafaka kasra|ini|ngaphambi|isiphetho salo / penultimate|futhi uma|kwaba|Inkathi yamanje|wafaka damma|okokuqala|wafaka fatha|ini|ngaphambi|isiphetho salo / penultimate.|Futhi ngithi:|okukhulunywa|umlobi|e|lezi|izimpawu|ka senza izinguquko eziningi|okuyinto|kwenzeka|e|igama eliyisenzo elithi|% nge-|ukusulwa|element yayo asebenzayo|futhi okunamathiselwe yayo|Iya ku-|the ayifeze,|nokuthi|ukuthi|IF|kwaba|igama eliyisenzo elithi|sikhatsi lesengcile|ibeka damma|yayo yokuqala|futhi ibeka kasra|incwadi|okuyinto|kungaphambi|isiphetho salo,|ke nina nithi:|(Yayisakazwa usike|igatsha)|futhi|(Yayisakazwa ngizazi ngekhanda|the isifundo)|futhi uma|kwaba|igama eliyisenzo elithi|Inkathi yamanje|ibeka damma|yayo yokuqala|futhi ibeka fatha|incwadi|okusho ukuthi|ngaphambi|isiphetho salo,|ke nina nithi:|(Wenziwa ukusika|igatsha)|futhi|(Wenziwa ngizazi ngekhanda|the isifundo).
